how beltan live within the greenwood


In glade forest yet far one might hear
chime bell steal across valley great minster
mortain still even dwelt beltan smith

alon live shadow great tree happi pipe
bird ear joy listen plash
murmur brook ran merrili besid hut paus twixt
stroke ponder hammer catch never fail music

mighti man beltan smith despit youth alreadi great
statur come featur much knew woodcraft growth
herb tree flower beast bird tell
cri song flight knew way fish stream
could tell cours star heaven vers
likewis ancient wisdom philosophi latin greek
learn thing men call ambros

way women less noth matter ambros spake
